Agents with different personas — educators, characters, support bots, creative agents — often shouldn&#39;t ask &#34;what do you want to do?&#34; because it implies they perform actions. An educator agent, for example, should ask an education-focused question, or not ask a question at all.\\n\\nOperators can try to override this via workspace files (SOUL.md, AGENTS.md), but because the hardcoded prompt is injected at the same level, the two instructions compete. The workspace instruction doesn&#39;t reliably win, leading to inconsistent greetings that break persona.\\n\\n### Proposed solution\\n\\nAdd a configurable session reset prompt in `openclaw.json`, e.g.:\\n\\n```json\\n{\\n  &#34;agents&#34;: {\\n    &#34;defaults&#34;: {\\n      &#34;sessionResetPrompt&#34;: &#34;A new session was started. Run your Session Startup sequence, then greet the user in your configured persona. Keep it to 1-3 sentences. Do not mention internal steps, files, tools, or reasoning.&#34;\\n    }\\n  }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nIf set, this replaces the hardcoded `BARE_SESSION_RESET_PROMPT_BASE`. If not set, the current default is preserved (backward compatible). Per-agent override via `agents.list[].sessionResetPrompt` would also be useful for multi-agent gateways where different agents need different greetings.\\n\\n### Alternatives considered\\n\\n- **Workspace file override** — currently attempted but unreliable because the hardcoded prompt competes at the same injection level. Not a clean solution.\\n- **Removing the greeting instruction entirely** — too disruptive; many agents benefit from the default. Making it configurable serves both cases.\\n\\n### Impact\\n\\n- **Affected:** Any operator running non-assistant agents (educators, characters, support bots, creative personas)\\n- **Severity:** Medium — persona breaks on every session start, visible to end users\\n- **Frequency:** Every session reset (daily resets, idle timeouts, manual /reset)\\n- **Consequence:** Inconsistent agent personality, operator has to repeatedly strengthen workspace instructions to fight the hardcoded prompt\\n\\n### Evidence/examples\\n\\nThe hardcoded prompt at `src/auto-reply/reply/session-reset-prompt.ts:4-5`:\\n\\n```typescript\\nconst BARE_SESSION_RESET_PROMPT_BASE =\\n  &#34;A new session was started via /new or /reset. Run your Session Startup sequence - read the required files before responding to the user. Then greet the user in your configured persona, if one is provided. Be yourself - use your defined voice, mannerisms, and mood. Keep it to 1-3 sentences and ask what they want to do. If the runtime model differs from default_model in the system prompt, mention the default model.
